contest-info 2022-11-06 16:11:15 ```diff
-ROTARY AIRCRAFT CONTEST-
``` 
**Objective:**
Build a Rotary Aircraft!

**Restrictions:**
-Your creation must be newly built. Submitting builds made before the contest will not be accepted. 
-You cannot use external programs for your build.
-Pixel art is off-limits.
-Staff members/event host reserve the right to delete contest submissions. 
-The vehicles you chose to build must include a rotor as their main source of lift (this includes tilt rotor aircraft, ornithopters, helicopters and any other rotor lifted VTOL) 
-Can NOT use helium or hover thrusters
-Be creative 

**Max submissions:**
2 Builds

**Submissions close on:**
December 6th, 9:00 PM (EST)


All contest submissions can be posted at contest-submissions  where they will then be posted in contest-creations to be voted on.  The winner will be determined through user vote. Only 1 winner will be chosen.
